  222 |     await page.getByRole('button', { name: 'Wall' }).click()
  223 |     await expect(page.locator('img[loading="lazy"]').first()).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10000 })
  224 |     await page.getByRole('button', { name: 'Map' }).click()
